pēllēi amaradattō, mittāṇaṁdō, paḍicchaē puraō । sā amaradatta karaghāyapēlliyā jāi ullaliuṁ ||67 ||1800||
tammi vaḍē ullaṁbiyamayapurisamuhammi jhatti pavisarai । unnaiyā taṁ daṭṭu mittāṇaṁdō suvimhaiō || 68 || 1801 ॥
hasai, taō maḍaēṇaṁ bhaṇiō ' mā hasasu thōvadiyahēhiṁ । ullaṁbiyassa tujjha vi ihēva naggōha sāhāē ॥ 69 ॥ 1802॥
pavisēhi muhammi duyaṁ aḍōliyā na'tthi ēttha saṁdēhō' । taṁ sōuṁ bhayabhīō sahasā ukkaṁpiō hiyaē ॥ 70 ॥ 1803 ॥
bhaṇai ya ' baccāmu gihaṁ', paḍibhaṇiō amaradatta kumarēṇa । 'kiṁ na ramijjai ?' 'līṇā maḍayamuhē jhaṭṭiyā ēsā ॥71॥ 1804 ॥ '
sō jaṁpai 'annā vihu amhāṇaṁ asthi ghicciyā rammā' । ' taha vi hu gammau gēhaṁ ' mittāṇaṁdēṇa paḍibhaṇiō ॥ 72 ॥ 1805 ॥
ēvaṁ ca amaradattō kīlāō niyattiuṁ gaō gēhaṁ । bhuttuttarammi puṇaravi miliyā tē dō vi varamittā ॥ 73 ॥ 1806 ॥
jā ubbiggaṁ pēcchai mittāṇaṁdaṁ taō bhaṇai iyarō । 'kiṁ mitta ! dīsasi tumaṁ kīyāṇa vi ukkiō caiva ॥ 74 ॥ 1807 ॥
kiṁ muṭuṁ tuha kēṇa vi savvassaṁ ?, vaṁciō vya kēṇā'vi ? । kiṁ vā kiṁpi virūvaṁ bhaṇiō kēṇā'vi duṭṭēṇa ? ॥ 75 ॥ 1808 ।।
kiṁ vā vi mayacchīē cittaṁ kīē vi avahiyaṁ tujjha ? । paribhaviō vā kēṇa vi ?, kiṁ vā maraṇassa bīhēsi ? ॥76॥ 1809 ॥
tā kahasu akahaṇīyaṁ jai navi' taṁ jaṁpaē taō ēsō । 'kiṁ mitta ! lavasi ēyaṁ aghaḍaṁta majjha visayammi ॥77॥ 1810 ॥
jēṇa pii - māi-bhagiṇī -bhajjā - bhāyāiyāṇa savvāṇa । kīrai jaṁpi rahassaṁ, na rahassaṁ taṁpi mittāṇa ॥ 78 ॥ 1811 ॥
1. pēllai ya ama° pā0 tru0 || 2. 'sālāē tru0 ।। 3. jhaḍḍhiyā kā0 । jhaṭṭiyā jē0 ।। 4. dhiṁciyā tru0 ||

kiṁtu maḍaēṇa tēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ maha sammuhaṁ imaṁ vayaṇaṁ । taṁ sumariūṇa cittaṁ bhaēṇa suṇṇattaṇaṁ vahai ॥79॥ 1812 ॥
bōllēi amaradattō 'na mayā kaiyāvi mitta ! jaṁpaṁti । vaṁtarakīlā ēsā kiṁ tu na yāṇijaē sammaṁ ॥ 80 ॥ 1813 ॥
kiṁ saccaṁ ciya ēyaṁ ? uyāhu hāsēṇa jaṁpiyaṁ tēṇa ? । tahavi hu purisāyārō purisēṇaṁ hōi kāvyō' ॥81॥ 1814 |
jaṁpai mittāṇaṁdō 'na purisayārēṇa sijjhaē kiṁpi । daivāyattē kajjē' vayai taō amaradattō vi ॥ 82॥ 1815 ।।
'kiṁ na suyaṁ akkhāṇaṁ tumaē kaiyāvi viusajaṇakahiyaṁ । purisāyārassa phalaṁ, jaha jāyaṁ nāṇagabbhassa' ॥83॥1816॥
iyarēṇa taō bhaṇiyaṁ 'kahēhi akkhāṇayaṁ imaṁ tāva' । bhaṇai imō 'vakkhēvaṁ vajrittu suṇāhi varamitta !' ॥84॥1817 ॥
"atyēttha bharahavāsē dhaṇa-dhanna samiddhibaṁdhurā nayarī । caṁpa tti suppasiddhā sāricchā alayanayarīē ॥1॥ 1818 ॥
taṁ bhuṁjai vararāyā jiyasattū nāma dasadisipayāsō । dariyārikuṁbhikuṁbhayaḍapāḍaṇē tikkhakharaṇaharō || 2 || 1819 ॥
tassa'tthi nāṇagabbhō maṁtī buddhīē vijiyaguru buddhī । nīsēsamaṁtimaṁḍalapamuhō vitthariyajasapasarō ॥ 3 ॥ 1820 ॥
tasya guṇāvalīē bhajjāē kucchisaṁbhavō jāō । puttō subuddhiṇāmō rūvī paccakkhamayaṇō vva ॥ 4 ॥1821॥
annē vi atthi puttā tīsē vinnāṇaguṇagaṇagghaviyā । aha nāṇagabbhamaṁtī nīsēsaṁ pālaē rajaṁ || 5 || 1822 ॥
jiyasattumahārannō kajjammi samujjaō sayā dhaṇiyaṁ । niyamaijiyapaṛivakkhō na gaṇai dariē vi paḍisattū ॥6॥1823॥
1. samaddhivaṁ tru0 vinā ||

paribhāviūṇa ēsō bhai taō 'dēva ! nāṇagabbhassa । hōhī mārī sakuṭuṁbayassa pakkhassa majjhammi' ॥ 16 ॥ 1833 ॥
taṁ sōūṇaṁ rāyā sapparisō vajratāḍiyasirō vva । uḍēuṁ niggacchai parisāō vimaṇadummaṇiō ||17|| 1834 ॥
maṁtī vi ya nēmitti hatthē gahiūṇa jāi niyagēhē । ēgaṁtagayaṁ sammāṇiūṇa paramēṇa viṇaṇa ||18|| 1835 ॥

tuha virahē maha ēyaṁ dhūlī - tiṇatullayaṁ va paḍihāi' । maṁtī vi āha ēvaṁ ēyaṁ natthēttha saṁdēhō ||30||1847॥
kiṁtu mahadhinimittaṁ rakkhijjau sāmi ! mā viyappēha' । rāyā vi hu paḍivajjiya ṭhāvai niyadidvivisayammi ।। 31 ।। 1848 ।।
pāhariyāī sutthaṁ kāuṁ paḍiyaggaē tisaṁjha pi । maṁtī vi cēiyagharē karēi aṭṭhāhiyāmahimaṁ ॥ 32॥1849 ॥

taṁ sōuṁ naranāhō jaṁpai 'pāvassa pēccha dudhariyaṁ । mattō vi jēṇa hatthī niyasuṁḍārakkhaṇaṁ kuṇai ||37|| 1854 ॥
tā mā kōi bhajau jaha kira rāyā asaṁgayaṁ kuṇai' । iya bhaṇiūṇa visajjai maṁtiviṇāsāya niyasēnnaṁ ।। 38 ।। 1855 ॥

akkhāē taṁ vāriya baccai sēṇāhivāṇa pāsammi । bhaṇai ya 'ōsaraha khaṇaṁ, jai maha sukayaṁ muṇaha kiṁpi ॥ 41 ॥1858 ॥

bhai ṇivō 'maha ēvaṁ acchariyaṁ kahasu mā vilaṁbēhi' । jaṁpai sō vi hu 'sāmiya ! maha kulakuddhēṇa kēṇā'vi ॥ 53 ॥1870 ॥

annaha ahaṁ pi sāmiya ! ṇa hu pattijjāmi ērisē kajjē' । pucchai rāyā 'kaha puṇa nāyaṁ ēyaṁ taē kajaṁ ? ' ॥ 55 ॥ 1872 ॥

mittāṇaṁdō jaṁpai 'ēvamiṇaṁ, kiṁtu tujjha aigaruyaṁ । duhaaṇuciyassa jāyai taṇḍuṇhāī mahādukkhaṁ ॥ 86 ॥ 1881 ॥

pāyāisōhaṇatthaṁ pavisittā tattha pavaravāvīē । pakkhāliyaṁgamaṁgā kōḍḍēṇa niyaṁti surabhavaṇaṁ ॥ 98 ॥ 1893 ॥
pēcchaṁtāṇa yacaḍiyā cittē aha amaradatta kumarassa । adubhaṁgaghaḍiyā puttaliyā sālabhaṁjīyā ॥ 99 ॥ 1894 ॥
taṁ pēcchatō kumarō ubbhaḍalāvaṇṇajōvvaṇaguṇaḍūḍhaṁ । uttuṁgathōrathaṇayaṁ varacchivicchōharamaṇijjaṁ ॥ 100 ॥ 1895 ॥

'vijayaṁtu dēvapāyā vijayaddhanariṁdavaṁdiyā ṇicaṁ । vararajñjasirīṇilayā dujjayariudappaṇiddalaṇā || 1 || 2656 ॥
vaddhāviha tumbhē, tiyasiṁda-nariṁdapaṇayapayajuyalō । bahusīsa - sīsiṇijuō jiṇidariddhīē dippatō ॥ 2 ॥2657॥

khaṁḍaṇa -pīsaṇa- raṁdhaṇa-payaṇa - virōlaṇapabhīi savvaṁ pi । ēyāē kāyavvaṁ' iya bhaṇiya visajaē taṁpi ॥ 53 ॥ 3282॥
ēvaṁ ciya taiyaṁ pi hu rakkhiyanāmaṁ pi pucchaī, sā vi । sāhai jahaṭṭhiyaṁ ciya, tattō tuṭṭhō bhai sēṭṭhī ॥ 54 ॥3283॥
bhaṁḍāgāriṇi ēsā hōu sayā majjha bhaṁḍayārammi । maṇi - mōttiya - vattha- suvaṇṇamāi āyattamēīē' ॥55॥3284 ॥
rōhiṇināmaṁ pitaō hakkārittā cautthiyaṁ suṇhaṁ । bhaṇai 'tumaṁ pi hu puttē ! appasu tē paṁca sālikaṇē' ॥56॥3285 ॥
tīē vi hu saṁlattaṁ ' bahusagaḍī - sāgaḍaṁ mahaṁ dēhi । vasabha - mahisāiyā vi ya jēṇaṁ appēmi tē sālī ' ॥57॥3286॥
bhaṇiyā ya sēṭṭhiṇā sā 'putti ! kahaṁ sāliakkhaē paṁca । bahusagaḍi - sāgaḍēṇaṁ nijjāijjati ? mē kahasu' ॥58॥3287 ॥
sāvitaō āīō kahai asēsa pi jaṁ jahāvihiyaṁ । sōūṇa tayaṁ sēṭṭhī ūsasiō nī makusumaṁ va ॥ 59 ॥ 3288 ॥

sō iha caiva bhavammiṁ bhaṇṇai lōēṇa duṭṭavayaṇēhiṁ । dhī ! dhī ! purāṇavayabharaparibhaggaciyāē lakkaḍaya ! ॥72॥3301॥

" atthi iha jaṁbudīvē vāsē ēravayanāmadhēyammi | viṁjhapuraṁ nāmēṇaṁ supasiddhaṁ puravaraṁ rammaṁ ॥ 1 ॥3350 ॥
tatthā''si viṁjhadattō rāyā puhaīē niggayapayāvō । sayalakalāpattaṭṭō rūvēṇaṁ kāmadēvō vva ॥2॥3351॥
tassā''si aggamahisī sulakkhaṇā nāma jōvvaṇaguṇaḍūḍhā । uttattakaṇayavaṇṇā accharasā caiva pañcakkhā ||3||3352॥
tīē ya samaṁ raṇṇō aṇidiyaṁ sōkkhamaṇuhavaṁtassa | dhamma'ttha- kāmasāraṁ tivaggasaṁpāyaṇasayahaṁ ॥4॥3353॥

nāmēṇa naliṇakēū, laliēṇaṁ tiyasakumarasāricchō । ummattajōvvaṇaḍūḍhō kāmiṇimaṇaharaṇavaracōrō || 6 || 3355॥
tō tatthēva purē baṁdhava kumuyāgarāṇa va sasaṁkō । āsi mahāyaṇasārō satthāhō dhammamittō tti ||7||3356 ॥
tassā''si varā bhajjā siridattānāma sayalaguṇakaliyā । tīsē ya āsi puttō dattō nāmēṇa supasiddhō || 8 ||3357॥
rūvēṇa raisaricchā, kaṁtīē rōhiṇi vva paccakkhā । sōhaggēṇaṁ gōri vba, tēyasā tiyasavilaya vva ॥ 9 ॥ 3358॥
pariṇīyā dattēṇaṁ pahaṁkarā nāma bhāriyā pavarā । tīē samaṁ sō bhōē bhuṁjai navajōvvaṇaḍḍhāē ||10||3359॥
aha annayā vasaṁtē parikaliō bhāriyāē sō dattō । bisaēsa mōhiyamaī ujjāṇē ramai līlāē ॥11॥3360॥
ēttō ya nailiṇikēū kumarō dahuṁ pahaṁkaraṁ sahasā । visamayasarassa pahārēhiṁ tāḍiō vacchadēsammi ॥12॥3361॥

ciṁtai maṇami ēvaṁ "ēsō ciya ēttha tihuyaṇē dhannō । jō ēīē samāṇaṁ ramai jahicchāē aṇavarayaṁ ॥ 13 ॥ 3362॥
tā kaha maha ēīē samayaṁ raisuharasāmayaṁ hōhī । ahavā kiṁ ciṁtāē ? nēmi imaṁ niyayagēhammi" || 14 | 3 363॥
iya ciṁtiūṇa ēsō dattasayāsāō hakkhuvēūṇa । rāyakumarattaṇēṇaṁ pahaṁkaraṁ nēi niyagēhē ॥ 15 ॥ 3364 ॥
bhuṁjai tīē samaṁ sō visayasuhaṁ niyamaṇammi parituṭṭhō । dattō vi tavbiōē ujjāṇē bhamai dukkhattō ॥ 16 ॥ 3365 ॥
hiṁḍatēṇa ya tahiyaṁ diṭṭhō sumaṇābhihāṇavarasāhū । pattō ya pāyamūlē jāva imō tassa sāhussa || 17||3366 ॥
sāyaṁ aṇataṁ uppaṇaṁ tassa kēvalaṁ nāṇaṁ । dēvā ya caunikāyā saṁpattā nāṇamahimāē ||18|| 3367॥
taṁ daṇaṁ dattō baṁda payapaṁkayaṁ muṇivarassa । dāūṇa dhammalābhaṁ muṇiṇā vi ya sāhiō dhammō ॥19॥ 3368 ॥
sōūṇa tayaṁ dattō uvasaṁtō dāṇadhammamāyarai । āukkhaēṇa mariuṁ uvavannō jaṁbudīvammi ॥20॥3369॥
vijayammi sukacchamma vēyaḍḍhē pavvayammi ramaṇīē । nayaraṁ suvaṇṇatilayaṁ atthi pasiddhaṁ surapuraṁ va ॥ 21 ॥3370॥
taṁ pālai vararāyā nāmēṇa mahiṁdavikkamō sūrō । tassa'tthi anilavēgā dēvī vijjāharapasiddhā ||22|| 3371॥
tāṇa suō sō dattō uppannō ajiyasēṇakayanāmō । bijāō sāhiūṇaṁ jāō vijāharakumārō ॥ 23 ॥ 3372 ॥
pariṇīyā tēṇa taō jōvvaṇapattēṇa rūva- guṇakaliyā । uttamakulasaṁbhūyā vijjāharabāliyā kamalā ||24||3373 ॥
tīē samaṁ vilasaṁtō bhuṁjai vijjāharubbhavē bhōgē । bhamai ya gayaṇayalēṇaṁ girivara- sari-kāṇaṇāīsu ॥ 25 ॥ 3374 ॥

iyarō vi naliṇakēū mayammi siriviṁjhadattarāyammi । āṇāmiyasāmaṁtō pālēi kamāgayaṁ rajaṁ ॥ 26 ॥ 3375 ॥
tīsē pahaṁkarāē raisuharasanivahapāṇadullaliō । dōgudugadēvō iva gayaṁ pi kālaṁ na yāṇāī ||27|| 3376 ॥
aha annayā kayāī pahaṁkarāē samaṁ samārūḍhō । varapāsāyatalammi pēcchai sōhaṁ puravarassa ||28||3377 ॥
ētyaṁtarammi gayaṇē samuggayā vivihavaṇṇa-rūbadharā । nayaṇa-maṇāṇaṁdayarā ghaṇanivahā disigaiṁda vva ॥ 29 ॥ 3378 ।।
bhiṁgaṁjaṇa-tāla-tamāla- gavala - alivalayasannihā kē vi । phaliṇī - kaṁdaladalacaya-kīracchavisacchahā annē ||30||3379॥
kiṁsuya-suyamuha- guṁjaddha- javaya- hiṁguluyaniyarasama kē vi । hariyālē bhēya-kaṁcaṇa kaṇiyāraya kusumasama annē ॥ 31 ॥3380 ॥
hima- hāra-phaliha-gōkhīra- kuṁda - phēṇakasappahā kē vi । uttuṁgagirivarā iva mēhā pūraṁti nahavivaraṁ ॥ 32॥3381॥
ghaṇagajiyabhariyaṇahā vijulayālōya kayacamakkārā । savvattō saṁchāiyadisivivarā nayaṇamōhaṇayā ॥ 33 ॥ 3382 ॥
daddr̥ṇaṁ tārisaē ghaṇaṇivahē harisaṇinbharō rāyā । savvattō avalōyai khaṇamēkkaṁ vimhiō jāba ||34||3383 ॥
tābē khara- pharusa - uddaṁḍapavaṇariṁchōlipēlliyā saṁtā । pēcchaṁtassēva ṇivassa jhatti addaṁsaṇīhūyā ||35|| 3 384 ॥
